DGE-LUGS-PA BI BLIOGRAPHICAL
NOTES



Se-ra Monastery: Ri khrod
Interview with Don-'grub-rdo-rje, 18 April, 1973
SE-RA BYES had the following hermitages:
1) Brag-ri Ri-khrod
2) Ke'u-tshang
3) Chu-bzang
4) Sgrub-khang
5) Phur-bu-lcog
6) Mkhar-rdo
7) Sman-mchog (nunnery)
8) Ga-ri (sp?) (nunnery)
The hermitages of SE-RA SMAD included:
1) Bkra-shis-chos-gling
2) 'Jog-po
3) Spang-lung

Ma ha
Bka' srung dam can Chos rgyal
Incipit:
/bskal bzang mam 'dren bzhi pa shākya'i tog/
Zrgyal tshab sa bcu'i dbang phyug mi pham mgon/
/rgyal kun mkhyen rab gcig bsdus 'jam dpal dbyangs/.
bka' drin mtshungs bral angos brgyud bla mar 'dud/
Zdge legs rin chen chu shel ba gam las/
Z'ong bas legs bshad 'od kyis 'gro rnams la/
Zsnang ba'i dpal sbyin bshes gnyen mtshan mo'i mgon/
mi 'bral spyi bo'i gtsug na rtag tu mchod/
mgon de'i thugs rje zla ba'i ma ma las/
/legs 'ong zab rgyas gdams zab bdud rtsi'i rgyun/
/bdag blo'i yol gor 'khyil rnams 'don sgrigs su/
rang mnyam gzhan la'ang phan phyir 'di na god/
/'dir skal ba dang idan pa'i gang zag thar pa dang thams cad
mkhyen par 'khrid pa'i thabs zab mo byang chub lam gyi rim
pa'i sngon 'gro sbyor ba'i chos drug nyams su len tshul la
gnyis/ thun gyi ngo bo la ji ltar bya ba dang/ thun mtshams
su ji ltar bya ba'i tshul lo/
Terminatur:
/ces byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i sngon 'gro sbyor ba'i
chos drug nyams su len tshui 'di ni/ rang gi sbyor chos khrid
lung bya skabs don gnyer can du mas rgyun khyer 'don sgrigs
su yod pa 'di lta bu zhig dgos zhes yang yang bskul ba la
brten nas sbyor chos thub bstan lhun po'i mdzes rgyan la
gzhir byas/ dam pa gong ma'i man ngag gis kha bskang ste
mkhyen yon pas sbyar ba'o/
Appended (ff. 12r-16r): Blo sbyor rtsa tshig dang don bdun
ma'i sa bcad sbrag nas nyung ngu'i tshig gis go bder bkral
ba.
Terminatur:
/zhes jo bo dang ston pa'i thugs dam blo sbyong rtsa
tshig sa dpyad dang sbrag nas go bder bkral ba bag chags
'jog phyir rjes sbyangs su mkhyen yon pas bkod pa'o/ /age
legs 'phel/
Bla ma mchod pa'i khrid yig dga' idan snyan rgyud man ngag
gter mdzod ces bya ba bzhugs so.
ff. 20
Margins: (r) Bla -- mchod
Incipit:
/'jam mgon bla ma'i thugs kyi gsang ba'i mdzod/
7snyan rgyud man ngag ma pi ka'i 'phreng ba/
Zspel mdzad grub mchog rgyal ba dben sa pa!
Zyab sras rgyud par bcas la snying nas "dud/
snyàn rgyud gdam zab srid pa'i sgron me la
Zsel med dpyad gsum dag pa'i lam drangs te
Zyid ches dad pa'i 'chi med lam yangs por/
gangs can skal bzang gdul bya'i dpal du char/

rgyal po tsong kha pa chen po'i thugs bcud/ grub mchog dharma
badzra yab sras kyi bka' srol/ skal ldan gyi skyes bu tshe



Lcang-rgyab Khri-chen
gcig sangs rgyas bsgrub pa'i myur lam bla ma mchod pa'i gsang
ba'i gnad mam par phye ba snyan rgyud man ngag gi gter mdzod
nyams su len pa la gsum/ gdams pa'i khung bshad pa/ gdams pa'i
che bad gdams pa dngos nyams su len tshul lo/...
rje thams cad mkhyen pas rtog ldan rin po che dang mkhas
grub rje la gnang/ sprul pa'i glegs bam rtogs ldan 'jam dpal
rgya mtsho'i phyag tu bzhugs/ rtog ldan rin po che snyan
rgyud gdam pa yongs rdzogs sprul pa'i glegs bam bcas ba so
chos rgyal la gnang/ des grub chen chos rdo rje la snyan
rgyud glegs bam bcas gnang nas dben par shin tu gsang bar
sgrub pa snying po bya dgos tshul gdams/ des rje dben sa pa
blo bzang don grub la gnang/ des mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye shes
la gnang/ des pan chen blo bzang chos rgyal la sprul pa'i
glegs bam bcas snyan rayud vongs rdzogs onang/ roval ba
rgyud yongs rdzogs gnang/ rgyal ba dben
sa par gzims ltas kyi tshul du lung bstan pa itar dus babs kyi/
pan chen blo bzang chos rgyal gyis 'jam mgon bka' srol thun
mong ma yin pa dben sa snyan rgyud kyi lam gyi lus yongs su
rdzogs pa'i bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga 'di mdzad nas skal idan
mtha' yas pa (f. 2v) la gnang nas/ gangs can gyi sa'i cha thams
cad la rje bla ma'i snyan rgyud kyi khyab par bka' drin
mdzad do/
/des rdo rje 'dzin pa akon mchog rgyal mtshan/ des pan
chen blo bzang ye shes la gnang/ des rdo rje'dzin pa blo
bzang rig grol la gnang/ des grub dbang blo bzang rnam rgyal
la gnang7 des tshe gling yongs 'dzin paņdi ta chen po la
gnang nas yongs 'dzin rin po ches dga' idan snyan rgyud man
ngag gter mdzod khrid yig rgyas 'bring sdus gsum mdzad de
so so'i rgyud rim bzhin da ita'i bar khyab brdal che bar
mdzad pa'i bka' drin bsam brjod kyi yul las 'das so/
Terminatur:
/ces pa 'di ni bla mchod bshad lung don gnyer can mang
po zhig la bya skabs/ dge bshes blo bzang ye shes sogs nas
da lan sa dpyad rnams bla mchod cho ga dang sgrags te khyer
bde ba zhig dgos tshul nan gyis bskul ba la brten nas dga' ldan
khri "dzin mkhyen yon pas sbyar ba'o/
mdo rgyud gdams pa'i dgongs don sa mu dra/
lung rigs dpyad gsum dag pa'i legs bsrub nas/
Zagos don snying po thabs shes nam mkha'i nor/
Zlus can skal idan yongs kyi dpal du shar/
'dir 'bad dge ba'i rnam akar la brten nas/
7rgyal bstan dar zhing de 'dzin sku tshe bsring/
Akhyad par 'jam mgon bla ma'i bshad sgrub bstan/
7mi nyams dbyar mtsho bzhin du rgyas gyur cig/ /sarba
mangga lam/
Bcom ldan 'das mam par snang mdzad rdo rje dbyings kyi bdag
mdun bum pa dbang chog smon shis bcas kyi cho ga nag 'gros
su bkod pa yid kyi re skong zhes bya ba bzhugs so.

rdo rje 'chang dang ye shes mkha' 'gro ma/

7gsol ba 'debs so dngos grub rnam gnyis stsol/
7shākya dpal bzang mkhas btsun sa gzhi dpal/
/dri med dpal bzang byang chub sengge dang/
skyo ston grags pa rgyal mtshan sher bzang la/
Igsol ba 'debs so X
tshul khrims rgyal ba byang sems chos kyi rgyal/ (f. lv)

mthu stobs abang gyur bzang po bkra shis la/
gsol ba 'debs so X
bkra shis dpal ldan mtshan dpe'i dbang gis rgyal/

Zphyag na padmo bskal bzang rgya mtsho dang/

/dga' ldan bstan'dzin ngag abang chos 'phel dang/
/grub pa'i dbang phyug blo bzang dar rgyas zhabs/
Akhri chen mkhyen rab yon tan rgya mtsho dpal/

Zihan skyes ye shes mtshan dpe'i skur shar ba/
/'gro la gcig tu phan pa'i longs spyod rdzogs (f. 2r)
/ngo mtshar rten dang brten par shar rnams la
/gsol ba 'debs so dngos grub rnam gnyis stsol
Zde Itar rtse gcig yid kyis gsol btab pas/
mchog thun dngos grub ma lus 'bad med du/
/thob cing rmad byung lam der rang nyid kyis/

gsol 'debs byas nas/...

ces shis pa brjod cing me tog gi char dbab par bya'o/

gyi cho ga dga' ldan stag rtse sgrub mchod du sngon nas
tshug mus yang/ bar skabs dbang bsnyen pa sogs ji bzhin ma
byung khar/ cho ga yang shin tu rgyas pas chog grwa rnams
kyi blos ma chun par dea' ldan tsha ba dang/ klu 'bum khang
mtshan gnyis nas khri thog gya brgyad pa mkhyen yon par
rdor abyings cho ga khung ldan/ dbang lung sogs 'jug pa bde
ba/ nyams pa sor chud yod pa zhig nan gyis bskul ba la
brten nas/ tshul 'di ni 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po dgung lo
nga dgu pa shing mo lug gi lor (A) dga' ldan yangs pa can
gtsug lag khang gsar du bskrun ċing/ gsang 'dus/ bde
mchog/ rdor abyings rnams kyi blos bslangs rje nyid kyi gsar

byung du byon pa dang/ rdor dbyings kyi rdo rje rgyal po/ rdo
rje chags pa gnyis las 'od zer 'phros par 'ja' tshon mar grags
pa dang/ rab tu gnas pa'i tshe rtags ngo mtshar can mang du

Lcang-rgyab Khri-chen
/'phung rỉ so sor brgyad brgyad dang/
/gnyen sa so bdun dgra ri dang/
sa gnam ri sgo dmigs bcu gnyis/
sa ro brgyad dang mtshon cha bzhi/ (bai dkar)
zur gsum kha dog ngan pa bcu/

la sogs sa dpyad le'u bzhin spong/

phye'i thig tshon cho ga khungs ldan khu bsdus kyi rang
gzhan yongs la phan phyir dga' ldan khri 'dzin mkhyen yon pas
bkod pa'o/

ba'i ril sgrub gzhan yang nyer mkho 'ga' zhig bcas bzhugs so.

/shing ma chu la shing bu me
chu ma lcags la chu bu shing
Alcags ma sa la lcags bu chu/
me ma shing la me bu sa/
sa ma me la sa bu lcags/
me dgra chu la me grogs lcags/
/chu dgra sa la chu grogs me/

par bya'o)

Blo-bzang-thugs-rje

Blo-bzang-thugs-rie
sna bsdus drag pa dang bcas dus phyis gnam bskos gzhung sa
mchog gi sku rim zhabs brtan ched dmigs su byang phyogs gdugs

dang bsnyen yig gzhan nas kyang kha bskang/ dam pa'i man ngag
dang mthong ba brgyud pa'i phyag len mam par dag pas kyang
brgyan te dpal ldan zla med dbus 'gyur rgyud grwa'i bsnyen
mtshams pa dag gis ngag 'don amigs rim phyag len dang bcas

de ltar gong du bkod pa de dag dkyus thog gcig la bshad
pa rdzogs par mdzad pa'i go skabs ma mchis mod kyang bshad
pa'i cha du mar phya ba dang skabs "brel gyi dbye bsdu'i sgo
sna tshogs dang (or: dad) phyir bshad pa bsdus pa'i mdzad
pa'i tshe yig chen gang yin dang/ de las kyang bsdu na ka thog
nas/ kha thog dang gcig thog nas gnyis thog tu len pa'i bsdu
lugs ci rigs dang/ yang bshad pa rgyas pa mdzad pa'i tshe yig
chen gyi steng du yig chung rams skabs'brel dang bstun ci
rigs blangs nas sbyar chog par bsam pas tshig tshogs ma skyungs
par skabs don gang 'brel mgo smos cha du ma nas bsdus te bkod
pa 'di yang mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag rgyud stod mkhan
chen nyid nas lo sngon ma (f. 20v) tsam nas rab gnas skabs kyi
bshad pa zhig bris zhes gsungs na'ang 'di dag ser smad khri
'dzin gyi go sa 'di bla gnyer sbrags ma'i 'brel g.yeng che
gshis bar bar zin bris thor bu btab pa tsam las dkyus gcig la
sgrigs long ma byung bar da bar lus kyang/ da lam mjug rdzogs

lags so/

Dge-lugs-pa literature
GSUNG-'BUM: ZHOGS-PA DON-YOD-MKHAS-GRUB (1671-1736)
Lha-sa Zhol (New) print in the possession of Gro-mo Dge-bshes Rin-po-
che; reprinted by Chatring Jansar Tenzin, 1974.
0. Rje btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang Don yod mkhas grub
rin po che'i gsung 'bum glegs bam gyi dkar chag bzhugs so.
ff. 3
Margins: (r) Dkar chag
7.3-7.6 x 50.5-51.0 T lines
Incipit:
/na mo gu ru ya/
snang stong zung 'jug yan lag bdun ldan sku/
/snyigs dus 'gro ba'i dpal du yongs shar ba
rdo rje 'chang chen don yod mkhas grub la/

gter chen por bzhugs kyang/ sngar yod 'bras spungs spar rnying
'gro don khyab gdal gyis bgres zad shin tu che bas gsung 'bum byings

bas gsar brko ma dgos par mkhas grub chen po lcang skya rol pa'i
rdo rje'i gsung 7 rgyal mchog nyid kyi mdzad rnam pod phyed gnyis
gsar bsnan dang boas te/ gsan yig ma gtogs pa'i gsung 'bum pod
brgyad yongs su rdzogs par/ rab byung bou drug pa'i shing bya lor

Skyid-shod Sprul-sku Ngag=dbang-bstan-'dzin-'phrin-las (1639-1682)
Incomplete manuscript in the possession of Bakula Rimpoche
1. Ka. Rdo rje sens dpa'i rjes gnang bya tshul bzhugs so.
ff. 6 (pp. 1-11)
Cf. MHTL 15121 (Rdor sems rjes gnang)

kyis nan tan chen pos bka' phebs pa Itar/ shākya'i btsun pa
ngag dbang bstan 'azin 'phrin las kyi bla ma gong ma'i gsung
rgyun ltar bkod pa'o/
2. Kha. Phreng ba gnyis kyi cho ga'i ngag 'don gyi rim pa 'khrigs
su sdebs pa mthong bas don grub zhes bya ba bzhugs so.
ff. 161 (pp., 13-333)
Cf. MHTL 15122 (Rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang chog ngag 'don
gyi rim pa mthong ba don 'grub)
/ces 'phreng ba gnyis kyi cho ga'i ngag 'don gyi rim pa
khrigsu sdebs pa mthong bas don grub ces pa 'di yang gangs
kyi ra bas yongs su bskor ba'i ljongs 'di'i rig sngags 'chang
mamsyi gtsug rgyan dam pa mkhas 'dus dpal ldan rgyud stod

Author: The Sixth Panchen Thub-bstan-chos-kyi-nyi-ma
/rmad byung bskal ba 'dzin mar stobs bcu'i rtsal/
/pha mthar son kyang gzhan don rjes chags pas/
bde can sems dpa'i tshul bzung 'gro ba'i mgon/
/phyag na pad dkar 'chang ba gtsug na rgyal/
mgon de'i thabs mkhas sgyu 'phrul rol ba'i gar/
sna tshogs gdul bya'i mos blo dang mtshungs pa/
ci yang char las che mchog 'dus pa rtsal/
byang chen ma thob de srid spyi bor mchod/
khyod nyid sa gsum yongs rdzogs zhi dang khro'i/
akyil 'khor ma lus spro zhing bsdu ba yi/
byed por nges rnyed de phyir lha 'ga' yi/
dag pa'i snang ba 'char la mtshar ci yod/
l'on kyang snyigs dus bdud dang dam sri yi/
log pa'i bsam sbyor phye marthag pa'i phyir/
7 gang 'dul 'phrin las rmad byung dus gsum mkhyen/
/padma ka ra'i (f. lv) ddongs zab nying khui beud/
ma sbas gsal rjen dngos nyams ci rigs par/
Z char ba'i legs bshad gsang ba'i rgya can gyi/
/nyams len bu yig ma 'dres dkar chag tshogs/
/mkha' 'gro'i snying gtam spel la gnang ba stsol/
de la 'dir chos kun ka dag gdod nas rang behin stong pa'i
dbyings las nam yang 'da' ba ma mchis kyang/ tha snyan rten 'brel
rol ba'i bkod pa mtha' klas pa dag 'ching 'dzin 'khrul ba'i kun
rtog gis bslang ba zhugs min gyi rjes su 'gro ldogs pas dag dang
ma dag gi skyon yod ci mchis 'char ba las/ gnyis spangs chen
po'i ye shes kyi rol par dag pa'i snang ba kho nar 'byams klas
pas sor rtogs ma mchis mod/ tshur mthong gdul bya mnams kyi mos
pa sna tshogs pas dkar min las mhta'i 'du (f. 2r) byed snyigs
ma'i rang mdangs mngon du gyur pa na/ gang dang gang nyid sdug
bsngal gyis nyam thag par gyur pa de dang de la shin tu brtse
ba'i thugs kyi 'jug pa skyong ba ni bdag nyid chen po rnams kyi
chos nyid lags pas7 dus mtha 'dir yang mi bzang pa'i gdung ba
sna tshogs pas gtsas pa'i 'gro ba rnams tshor ba de las bskyab
pa'i phyir dang/ ris med rgyal bstan nag phyogs pa rud rigs kyis
tshe ba'i dngos po las grol phyiri rgyal ba kun 'dus mtsho
skyes rdo rjes sngon gyi dam bca' nye bar 'gongs te gang 'dul
'phrin las kyi rol pa rmad du byung ba gang la 'jug pa'i gzhi/
phyag na pad dkar 'chang ba sdom brtson rgyal po'i mam par rol
ba snyigs dus kyi pandi ta ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtshor
dngos nyams sna tshogs par slob dpon chen po rang nyid kyis
mtshon bka' gter grub mchog du mas nye brgyud kyi tshul du
'doms par mdzad pa'i zab chos snod min mnams la gsang ba'i slad
du mtshan ma ci rigs pa'i rgyas mongs su gtams pa'i gzigs snang
rgya can du grags pa'i chos skor la dus babs (f. 2v) lung du
bstan pa sogs dngos gzhi dang/ de'i cha lag 'phrin las kyi rim
pa gsal bar nag 'gros su bkod pa ste/ ma yig bu yig gi tshul
du bzhugs pa las/ bu yig grangs rags rim lcang lung pandi ta'i
phyag dpe'i khrod gang bzhugs rnams la ma dpe byas te gsar 'drir
bcug pa'i dkar chag mkha' 'gro'i snying gter bkod pa la)
//gtan deb kyi 'go brjod shing phag (1934) zla tshes dge ba
la/
/bgrang yas sngon nas tshad med snying brtse'i gter/



/mtha' yas goms pas rtsod Idan 'gro tshogs la/
/bgrang yas bdud rtsi'i bgo bsha' sbyin mdzad pa/
mtha' yas 'gro mgon shākya sengger dud/
7snyoms thugs bde chen chos dbyings mdzes ma la/
Zdam du 'khyud pas zung 'jug mchog bryes kyang
rgyal sras tshul bzung thub gsung mdzod 'dzin pa/
Z'jam dbyangs bla mas shes rab spobs pa stsol/
chos kun gnas lugs ma 'dres snyan pa'i gdangs/
mkhyen yangs sor rtse'i 'phrul gyis rgyud mang glur/ (f.
3r) bkug ste skal bzang rna ba'i bcud kyi dpal/
sbyin mkhas mtsho byung lha mos rtag tu skyongs/
Zyul gyis bskal yang rjod byed chig gi dbyangs/
nye bar gnas bzhin ji lta ji snyed kyi/
gnas tshul rjen par 'char ba'i 'phrul gyi sgo/
phye slad yi ge'i 'phreng ba 'di na spel/
gang dag sde bzhi'i dpal yen kun rdzogs pa'i/
rgyal thabs bya ba mnam dpyod phrag pa yis/
/khur du 'khyer la brtson pa lhod min pa'i/
Zgzhon nu'i tshogs kun spyan akyus yangs par phye/
7zhes pa 'di yang 7 shākya'i dge sbyong blo bzang thub bstan
chos kyi nyi mas so/

Zdab stong ge sar dpal yon snying po'i boud/
Zyongs bltams mtsho skyes rdo rje zhes grags pa'i/
mtshan snyan utpal 'phreng mdzes dus gsum mkhyen/
7snyigs dus 'gro ba'i skyabs mchog gang des skyongs/
rdo rje'i lus la gnad du bsnun gyur pas/

na mah shri kā li de wi ya/
/rab 'byams rgyal kun 'khor lo'i rgyan gyi gzugs/
/thabs mkhas sgyu 'phrul cir yang rol pa'i gar/
spro bsdu'i byed po rdo rje'dzin pa'i gtso/
/blo bzang bstan 'dzin dbang rgyal gtsug tu rgyal/
/rgyal kun yum gyur dbyangs can ngag gi lha/
/bstan dgra 'dul phyir drag mo'i skur bzhengs pa/
7'dod khams kyi dbang phyug re ma tis/
Zrjes chags brtse ba'i 'khyud chos rtag tu skyongs/
/gang gi mam bzhi'i 'phrin las dge mtshan dpal/ (f.lv)
/ gugs phyir bsnyen sgrub mchod gtor las kyi rim
thun mong thun nong min pa'i mạm gzhag tshoes/
Zgsal bar ston pa'i man ngag be'u bum/
/rgyud dang rgya bod mkhas grub gsung gi bcud/
/tshad 1dan gcig tu bsdus pa'i puşta kah/
ma nor gsal bar phye ba'i dkar chag phreng/
7spel la chos bdag mkha' 'gros gnang ba rtsol/.
Zde la 'dir ngag abang sgra dbyangs lha mo snyigs dus bstan
dgra 'dul phyir gtum drag rol pa'i skur bzhengs pa dpal ldan dmag
zor rgyal mo 'di nyid gsang sngags gsar (f. 2r) mying mtha' dag
pas bsten cing bsgrub pa'i srung ma'i gtso bor bzung zhing/ khyad
par du yang bkra shis lhun gyis grub pa'i chos grwa chen po 'di
nyid pad akar 'chang abang thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub pa
dpal bzang pos thog mar phyag 'debs pa'i dus su'ang lha mchog 'di
nyid la sgos kyi gnyer gtad mdzad pa dang/ de rjes bde ldan zhing
mgon ma ha pandi tablo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan nas bzung sku
phreng dang/mkhan slob rim par byon pa thams cad kyis kyang srung
ma'i gtso bor mdzad pas rang cag rjes su 'jug pa mtha' dag gis
kyang tshul bzhin du bsten nas phrin las myur mgyogs che ba bcas/
bdag nyid kyis kyang bka' drin 'khor zla med pa yongs 'dzin (f. 2v)
rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs drung nas 'di nyid kyi thun mong
dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba'i rim pa rdzogs par
ranos shing/ rgyun gyi mchod gtor sogs la 'bad pa skyed bzhin yang/
'di'i be'u bum cha tshang ba sngar phan lag tu ma son khar/ le
mtshan kha yar son pa la'ang chos skyong 'di nyid gsar sngags
gsar mying/ bon lugs/ dge lugs pa sogs grub mtha' ris med kyis
bsten gshis chos skor la'ang bsre lhad kyi 'phros pa mang bas yid
brtan dka' ba bcas rimlus su gyur pa da lam lcang lung pandi ta'i
dgon por bskyod sdod skabs lcang lung ārya pandi ta sku 'phreng
gong ma ngag dbang blo bzang (f. 3r) bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po'i gzims chung phyag dpe'i khrod du be'u bum phyogs bsdebs
cha tshang zhig 'dug par phyi mo byas te gsar "drir bcug pa 'di'i
nang gtso bor rgyud dang rgya gzhung rje dge 'dun grub pa dpal
bzang pos phyogs bsgrigs mdzad pa'i chos skyong yongs rdzogs/
ma hā pandi ta rdo rje thogs med rtsal gyi dag snang 'khor lo'i
rgya can gyi las sna tshogs/ rje bzhad pa rdo rjes mdzad pa'i
chos skor rnams kyang phyag na padmo thams cad mkhyen pa skal
bzang rgya mtshos khung idan du bzhed pas de skar yongs rdzogs/
rje gong ma rnam gnyis sogs rang re dge ldan ring lugs 'dzin pa'i
bla ma gong ma'i gsung bka' rgya mar gtogs pa 'ga' zhig bcas
'khod pa'i be'u bum 'di nyid kyi bsnyen sgrub las so sor phye ste

7) Beg tse'i 'khor lo kha sbyor las pho 'khor mo 'khor bzhugs
las sbyor pho 'khor mo 'khor 'di khyab bdag gnas gsar ba'i.

tsha mkhan chen mthu stobs dpal 'byor nas bdag za hor ban dhe'i
lag du son pa'i khyad chos lags sho.

Beg tse be'u bum
CHI
na mo gu ru bhyoh gnod sbyin shan pa lcam sring gi chos skor
byung tshul ni bcom idan 'das 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed pos a tsa
ra nyi ma grags la gnang/ des kho rang gi sras pandi ta zla ba
nag po la mang den kho rang say ga ya Cha ra la nang khong la
bod na mtshan gsum ste/ ga ya dha ra zhes kyang bya/ a tsa ra amar
po zhes kyang bya/ shri dha ra kra shu zhes kyang ba'o/
khong gis gnyan lo tstsha ba la gnang/ des gnam kha'u pa la
gnang/ des bla chen kun (f. 529) dga' snying po, la gnang/ des khong
gi nye gras shud' pu bkra shis 'od zer la gnang/ des grub thob "dar
char la gnang ba'o/
/yang lugs goig la/ shri dha ra kra shu mar pa lo (lho brag
dang ma gcig go) tsha la abus kyi grwa thang du gnang zhing dpe
mnams bsgyur/
gtsang du cog ro zangs ma'i bandhe ra ma skyabs la gnang/
gung thang du bon po gcig la gnang/
de Itar dngos slob bzhi byung zhing/
bandhe dar ma skyabs kyis slar yang mar pa lotstsha la gsan
pa yin la/ khong la shud bu bkra shis 'od zer gyi zhus/ de la
dar char gyi zhus pa lags so/
/yang lugs i la/ nags rgyal lha chu'i brag phug gong mar
slob dpon padma dngos su byon nas/ grub thob 'dar char la gnang
ste/ grub thob 'dar char la gnyan lo nas brgyud pa dang/ mar pa
nas brgyud pa dang/ slob dpon padma nas brgyud pa ste/ de gsum ka
nas brgyud pa'i rjes gnang man ngag tshang na mga' la, khong gi
bo tong rin po che brtson 'grus rdo rje 'chang la gnang/ des jo
sras sangs rgyas rin chen la gnang/ des slob apon shes rab rgya
mtsho la gnang/ des bla ma bsod nams dbang, phyug la gnang/ de nas
bla ma spyang se ba seng ge 'bum la grang) (f. 53r)
des kun mkhyen mu srad pa dpal idan sengge la gnang/ des mam
grol ba rin chen bkra shis la gnang/ des chos rje yon tan mgon po
la gnang/ des stag sde dgon gsar gyi mkhan po la gnang/ des bla
chen rdo rje rgyal mtshan la gnang/
yang bo tong rin poches nyan chen pa la gnang/ des mkhan po
chos rgyal dpal bzang po/ des bla ma bsam pa la gnang/ des bla
ma bsam 'grub bzang po la/ des rin po che rdo rje rgyal mtshan la/
des bdag gnyags kyi bandhe (mus chen) la/ chos skor tshang bar
gnang ba legs soſ
J'ai lta bu'i bla ma dam pa thams cad kyang bsrungs ma 'di
nyid la mga' brnyes shing mthu che ba grags tel a tsa ra nyi ma
grags pas mig bltas tsam gyis dgra 'chi/ pandi ta zla ba nag po
khros pa tsam gyis dgra 'chi/ ga ya dha ra sa zhagsum gyi las
sbyor byas pas dgra 'chi/ bla ma gnyan los ni mgon po zhal bzhi
pa'i las mkhan shan pa dmar nag tu grags te shin tu gnyan zhing reg
thabs med par grags la/ bandhe dharma skyabs kyis dgra thams cad
rjes med par gtang/ shud bu bkra shis 'od zer gyi dgra la rtags
yang yang thon/ grub thob 'dar char gyis bon po'i sde mang po
tshar (f. 53v) bcad/
mdor na bla ma gong ma rnams kyis chos skyong 'di'i sgo nas
grub pa'i rtags mang du bton pa sha stag lags so/
bsrungs ma 'di bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed kyi gsung gi
sprul pa yin la/ dpal rta mgrin gyi thugs kyi sprul par yang bla
ma gong ma 'ga' zhig gis bzhed cing/ gnod sbyin chen por tshul
bzung nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsrung zhing/ zhing bcu sgrol
ba'i las mdzad pa yin no/ 'di la chos skyong gi mthil du byas na
longs spyod shin tu che ba dang/ mthu mno la myur ba yang nges
par 'dug gsungs/ bla ma rnams kyi gsung sgros lo rgyus gnyags kyi
bandes yi ger bkod pa'o/
